. *Create share of females in village and census data (variables indicated with census_*)

(11 missing values generated)
. gen census_caste_females_share = census_caste_females/census_caste_total
(52 missing values generated)
. gen census_tribes_females_share = census_tribes_females/census_tribes_total
(12 missing values generated)
. label var census_pop_females_share "Share of females in the village based on census data"
. label var census_caste_females_share "Share of female scheduled castes population in the village based on census data"
. label var census_tribes_females_share "Share of female scheduled tribes population in the village based on census data"
. 
. *Share of women and men in sessions
. gen share_leader_female_vill = leader_female_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_female_vill = no_leader_female_vill/14 
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_leader_male_vill = leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_male_vill = no_leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. label var share_leader_female_vill "Share of female leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_female_vill "Share of women per session"
. label var share_leader_male_vill "Share of male leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_male_vill "Share of men per session"
. 
. * Games were discussed outside the workshop?
. gen com_outside_game =.
(83 missing values generated)
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_oth==1
(4 real changes made)
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_inf_family==1 
(34 real changes made)
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_Comm_meet==1 
(18 real changes made)
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_VC_meet==1 
(1 real change made)
. label var com_outside_game "=1 if games were discussed in formal or informal meetings in the village"
. 
. *recode shares to either dummies () or percent
. *share of women participating in games
. gen share_female_percent = share_female_village*100
(27 missing values generated)
. *presence of illiterate participants
. gen d_illiterate = 0 if share_illiterate_village==0
(50 missing values generated)
. replace d_illiterate = 1 if share_illiterate_village>0 & share_illiterate_village!=.
(23 real changes made)
. *share of leaders present in games
. gen share_leader_percent = share_leader_vill*100
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_leader_opt_percent = share_lead_opt_r9_10*100
(27 missing values generated)
. 
. *replace missing values with median values
. replace game_lead_facil = 0 if village_id==13 // who was lead facilitator in Dhamangoan?
(1 real change made)
. replace com_outside_game = 0 if village_id==17
(1 real change made)
. replace count_intervention = 26 if village_id==13 // when were the games played in Dhamangoan?
(1 real change made)
. 
. 
. egen bs_any_conflict = rowmax(BS_Confl_dam_ BS_Confl_distr_ BS_Confl_maint_ BS_Confl_oper_)
. 
. replace come_back_dummy = . if treatment==0
(27 real changes made, 27 to missing)
. 
. }

. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in % including female leaders"
variable share_female_percent2 not found
r(111);
. gen share_female_percent2 = share_no_leader_female_vill*10
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in %"
. gen share_female_percent3 = share_no_leader_female_vill*10
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in 10%"
. 
. gen leader_present = 0
. replace leader_present = 1 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==0
. replace leader_present = 2 if leader_female_vill == 0 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = 3 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = . if treatment==0
. lab def leader_lab 0 "None" 1 "Female" 2 "Male" 3 "Both", replace
. lab val leader_present leader_lab
. tab leader_present, gen(leader_)
. 
. gen leader_present2 = 0 if leader_present==0
. replace leader_present2 = 1 if leader_present==2
. replace leader_present2 = 2 if leader_present==1 | leader_present==3
. lab def leader_lab2 0 "None" 1 "Only male" 2 "Only female or both", replace
. lab val leader_present2 leader_lab2
. tab leader_present2, gen(leader2_)
. 
.

. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_oth==1
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_inf_family==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_Comm_meet==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_VC_meet==1

.

.

. *--------------------------------------------------------------------------
. * SCRIPT: 01_cleangen.do
. * PURPOSE: cleans data from the surveys
. *--------------------------------------------------------------------------
. 
. *----------------------------
. * 1) Load dataset downloaded from SoSci
. use "$working_ANALYSIS/data/data_merged.dta", clear

. 
. *----------------------------
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. *----------------------------
. * 1. GENERATE
. {
. *Create share of females in village and census data (variables indicated with census_*)
. gen census_pop_females_share = census_population_females/census_population_total
(11 missing values generated)
. gen census_caste_females_share = census_caste_females/census_caste_total
(52 missing values generated)
. gen census_tribes_females_share = census_tribes_females/census_tribes_total
(12 missing values generated)
. label var census_pop_females_share "Share of females in the village based on census data"
. label var census_caste_females_share "Share of female scheduled castes population in the village based on census data"
. label var census_tribes_females_share "Share of female scheduled tribes population in the village based on census data"
. 
. *Share of women and men in sessions
. gen share_leader_female_vill = leader_female_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_female_vill = no_leader_female_vill/14 
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_leader_male_vill = leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_male_vill = no_leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. label var share_leader_female_vill "Share of female leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_female_vill "Share of women per session"
. label var share_leader_male_vill "Share of male leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_male_vill "Share of men per session"
. *share of women participating in games
. gen share_female_percent = share_female_village*100
(27 missing values generated)
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in % including female leaders"
variable share_female_percent2 not found
r(111);
. gen share_female_percent2 = share_no_leader_female_vill*100
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in %"
. gen share_female_percent3 = share_no_leader_female_vill*10
. lab var share_female_percent3 "Share female participants in 10%"
. 
. gen leader_present = 0
. replace leader_present = 1 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==0
. replace leader_present = 2 if leader_female_vill == 0 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = 3 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = . if treatment==0
. lab def leader_lab 0 "None" 1 "Female" 2 "Male" 3 "Both", replace
. lab val leader_present leader_lab
. tab leader_present, gen(leader_)
. 
. gen leader_present2 = 0 if leader_present==0
. replace leader_present2 = 1 if leader_present==2
. replace leader_present2 = 2 if leader_present==1 | leader_present==3
. lab def leader_lab2 0 "None" 1 "Only male" 2 "Only female or both", replace
. lab val leader_present2 leader_lab2
. tab leader_present2, gen(leader2_)
. 
. 
. * Games were discussed outside the workshop?
. gen com_outside_game =.
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_oth==1
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_inf_family==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_Comm_meet==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_VC_meet==1 
. label var com_outside_game "=1 if games were discussed in formal or informal meetings in the village"
. 
. *recode shares to either dummies () or percent
. 
. *presence of illiterate participants
. gen d_illiterate = 0 if share_illiterate_village==0
. replace d_illiterate = 1 if share_illiterate_village>0 & share_illiterate_village!=.
. *share of leaders present in games
. gen share_leader_percent = share_leader_vill*100
. gen share_leader_opt_percent = share_lead_opt_r9_10*100
. 
. *replace missing values with median values
. replace game_lead_facil = 0 if village_id==13 // who was lead facilitator in Dhamangoan?
. replace com_outside_game = 0 if village_id==17
. replace count_intervention = 26 if village_id==13 // when were the games played in Dhamangoan?
. 
. 
. egen bs_any_conflict = rowmax(BS_Confl_dam_ BS_Confl_distr_ BS_Confl_maint_ BS_Confl_oper_)
. 
. replace come_back_dummy = . if treatment==0
. 
. }
r(111);

end of do-file

. *--------------------------------------------------------------------------
. * SCRIPT: 01_cleangen.do
. * PURPOSE: cleans data from the surveys
. *--------------------------------------------------------------------------
. 
. *----------------------------
. * 1) Load dataset downloaded from SoSci
. use "$working_ANALYSIS/data/data_merged.dta", clear

. 
. *----------------------------
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. *----------------------------
. * 1. GENERATE
. {
. *Create share of females in village and census data (variables indicated with census_*)
. gen census_pop_females_share = census_population_females/census_population_total
(11 missing values generated)
. gen census_caste_females_share = census_caste_females/census_caste_total
(52 missing values generated)
. gen census_tribes_females_share = census_tribes_females/census_tribes_total
(12 missing values generated)
. label var census_pop_females_share "Share of females in the village based on census data"
. label var census_caste_females_share "Share of female scheduled castes population in the village based on census data"
. label var census_tribes_females_share "Share of female scheduled tribes population in the village based on census data"
. 
. *Share of women and men in sessions
. gen share_leader_female_vill = leader_female_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_female_vill = no_leader_female_vill/14 
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_leader_male_vill = leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. gen share_no_leader_male_vill = no_leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)
. label var share_leader_female_vill "Share of female leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_female_vill "Share of women per session"
. label var share_leader_male_vill "Share of male leaders per session"
. label var share_no_leader_male_vill "Share of men per session"
. *share of women participating in games
. gen share_female_percent = share_female_village*100
(27 missing values generated)
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in % including female leaders"
variable share_female_percent2 not found
r(111);
. gen share_female_percent2 = share_no_leader_female_vill*100
. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in %"
. gen share_female_percent3 = share_no_leader_female_vill*10
. lab var share_female_percent3 "Share female participants in 10%"
. 
. gen leader_present = 0
. replace leader_present = 1 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==0
. replace leader_present = 2 if leader_female_vill == 0 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = 3 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==1
. replace leader_present = . if treatment==0
. lab def leader_lab 0 "None" 1 "Female" 2 "Male" 3 "Both", replace
. lab val leader_present leader_lab
. tab leader_present, gen(leader_)
. 
. gen leader_present2 = 0 if leader_present==0
. replace leader_present2 = 1 if leader_present==2
. replace leader_present2 = 2 if leader_present==1 | leader_present==3
. lab def leader_lab2 0 "None" 1 "Only male" 2 "Only female or both", replace
. lab val leader_present2 leader_lab2
. tab leader_present2, gen(leader2_)
. 
. 
. * Games were discussed outside the workshop?
. gen com_outside_game =.
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_oth==1
. replace  com_outside_game = 0 if FS_Shar_exp_inf_family==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_Comm_meet==1 
. replace  com_outside_game = 1 if FS_Shar_exp_oth_mem_VC_meet==1 
. label var com_outside_game "=1 if games were discussed in formal or informal meetings in the village"
. 
. *recode shares to either dummies () or percent
. 
. *presence of illiterate participants
. gen d_illiterate = 0 if share_illiterate_village==0
. replace d_illiterate = 1 if share_illiterate_village>0 & share_illiterate_village!=.
. *share of leaders present in games
. gen share_leader_percent = share_leader_vill*100
. gen share_leader_opt_percent = share_lead_opt_r9_10*100
. 
. *replace missing values with median values
. replace game_lead_facil = 0 if village_id==13 // who was lead facilitator in Dhamangoan?
. replace com_outside_game = 0 if village_id==17
. replace count_intervention = 26 if village_id==13 // when were the games played in Dhamangoan?
. 
. 
. egen bs_any_conflict = rowmax(BS_Confl_dam_ BS_Confl_distr_ BS_Confl_maint_ BS_Confl_oper_)
. 
. replace come_back_dummy = . if treatment==0
. 
. }
r(111);

end of do-file

. *--------------------------------------------------------------------------
. * SCRIPT: 01_cleangen.do
. * PURPOSE: cleans data from the surveys

. 
. *----------------------------
. * 1) Load dataset downloaded from SoSci
. use "$working_ANALYSIS/data/data_merged.dta", clear

.

. 
. 
. 
. 
.

. * 1. GENERATE
. 
. *Create share of females in village and census data (variables indicated with census_*)
. gen census_pop_females_share = census_population_females/census_population_total
(11 missing values generated)

. gen census_caste_females_share = census_caste_females/census_caste_total
(52 missing values generated)

. gen census_tribes_females_share = census_tribes_females/census_tribes_total
(12 missing values generated)

. label var census_pop_females_share "Share of females in the village based on census data"

. label var census_caste_females_share "Share of female scheduled castes population in the village based on census data"

. label var census_tribes_females_share "Share of female scheduled tribes population in the village based on census data"

. 
. *Share of women and men in sessions
. gen share_leader_female_vill = leader_female_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)

. gen share_no_leader_female_vill = no_leader_female_vill/14 
(27 missing values generated)

. gen share_leader_male_vill = leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)

. gen share_no_leader_male_vill = no_leader_male_vill/14
(27 missing values generated)

. label var share_leader_female_vill "Share of female leaders per session"

. label var share_no_leader_female_vill "Share of women per session"

. label var share_leader_male_vill "Share of male leaders per session"

. label var share_no_leader_male_vill "Share of men per session"

. *share of women participating in games
. gen share_female_percent = share_female_village*100
(27 missing values generated)

. lab var share_female_percent "Share female participants in % including female leaders"

. gen share_female_percent2 = share_no_leader_female_vill*100
(27 missing values generated)

. lab var share_female_percent2 "Share female participants in %"

. gen share_female_percent3 = share_no_leader_female_vill*10
(27 missing values generated)

. lab var share_female_percent3 "Share female participants in 10%"

. 
. gen leader_present = 0

. replace leader_present = 1 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==0
(11 real changes made)

. replace leader_present = 2 if leader_female_vill == 0 & leader_male_vill==1
(17 real changes made)

. replace leader_present = 3 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==1
(2 real changes made)

. replace leader_present = . if treatment==0
(27 real changes made, 27 to missing)

. lab def leader_lab 0 "None" 1 "Female" 2 "Male" 3 "Both", replace

. lab val leader_present leader_lab

. tab leader_present, gen(leader_)

      Total |         56      100.00

(57 missing values generated)

. replace leader_present2 = 1 if leader_present==2

(27 missing values generated)

. lab var share_female_percent3 "Share female participants in 10%"

.

. replace leader_present = 2 if leader_female_vill == 0 & leader_male_vill==1
(17 real changes made)

. replace leader_present = 3 if leader_female_vill == 1 & leader_male_vill==1
(2 real changes made)

. replace leader_present = . if treatment==0
